      <h2>
       <span>
        Occupation: Girl
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span>
        Please close the door and switch on the fun without fail.
       </span>
      </h3>
     </div>

      <div class="content-inner">

         </dt>
         <dt class="entry-title">
          Oh, why the hell not?
          <a href="http://cleolinda.livejournal.com/768604.html" rel="bookmark" style="display:none;">
          </a>
         </dt>
         <dd class="entry-text">
          <dl class="vcard author">
           <dt>
            <img alt="marie yum" height="100" src="http://l-userpic.livejournal.com/67581635/1427760" width="100"/>
           </dt>
           <dd class="username">
            <span class="ljuser i-ljuser i-ljuser-type-P " lj:user="cleolinda">
             <a class="i-ljuser-profile" href="http://cleolinda.livejournal.com/profile" target="_self">
              <img class="i-ljuser-userhead" src="http://l-stat.livejournal.net/img/userinfo.gif?v=17080?v=128.7"/>
             </a>
             <a class="i-ljuser-username" href="http://cleolinda.livejournal.com/" target="_self">
              <b>
               cleolinda
              </b>
             </a>
            </span>
           </dd>
           <dd class="entry-date">
            <abbr class="updated" title="2009-04-22T20:54:00+03:00">
             April 22nd, 2009
            </abbr>
           </dd>
          </dl>
          <div class="metadata">
           <dl class="meta-mood">
            <dt class="meta-mood-label">
             Current Mood:
            </dt>
            <dd class="meta-mood-value">
             <img alt="amused" class="meta-mood-img" src="http://l-stat.livejournal.net/img/mood/twotone/hamsters/giggly_hammy.gif"/>
             amused
            </dd>
           </dl>
          </div>
          <div class="entry-content">
           So I had some time to kill while I was waiting on multiple batches of cookies to bake (another thing for Mom's work), and
           <span class="ljuser i-ljuser i-ljuser-type-P " lj:user="starherd">
            <a class="i-ljuser-profile" href="http://starherd.livejournal.com/profile" target="_self">
             <img class="i-ljuser-userhead" src="http://l-stat.livejournal.net/img/userinfo.gif?v=17080?v=128.7"/>
            </a>
            <a class="i-ljuser-username" href="http://starherd.livejournal.com/" target="_self">
             <b>
              starherd
             </b>
            </a>
           </span>
           sent me a spare pack of those Twilight conversation heart candies, which
           <a href="http://cleolinda.livejournal.com/764742.html">
            I had said I should just go ahead and review.
           </a>
           You know. For science! Besides, a different movie site writes about these every two weeks and then everyone sends me the link so, you know: The Official Discussion of Nasty-Ass Colored Chalk Candy. Let it be so.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Note: I would be more than happy to do this with candy or merchandise from another fandom (I still kind of regret not getting the Pirates of the Caribbean cereal, actually). Except Bertie Botts' Every Flavor Beans. I ain't tastin' no earwax candy. My dedication only goes so far, people.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <a name="cutid1">
           </a>
           <br/>
           <div style="text-align:center">
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017pg55/">
             <img src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017pg55/s320x320"/>
            </a>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017rtcp/">
             <img src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017rtcp/s320x320"/>
            </a>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017q984/">
             <img src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017q984/s320x320"/>
            </a>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017sx72/">
             <img alt="" src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017sx72/s320x320" width="300"/>
            </a>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017tq46/">
             <img alt="" src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017tq46/s320x320" width="300"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           The pictures do not do the box itself justice--I had a really hard time getting a shot with accurate color, which is important because poor RPattz looks like he wants your braaaaaains, not your blood. Here's the best I could do with color correction:
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="text-align:center">
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/00180wab/">
             <img alt="" src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/00180wab/s320x320" width="200"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Because when I want to sell you candy, I think "greenish leper."
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="text-align:center">
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017wfzc/">
             <img src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017wfzc/s320x320"/>
            </a>
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017x5tk/">
             <img alt="" height="240" src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017x5tk/s320x320"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           These are the only legible hearts in the entire package. Yes, the whole thing. But what do they say?
           <br/>
           <br/>
           "Does that say 'lame'?"
           <br/>
           <br/>
           "No,
           <em>
            lamb--
           </em>
           "
           <br/>
           <br/>
           "What was lamb?"
           <br/>
           <br/>
           "Mom, you saw the movie! You know! The part with the lion and the lamb and--"
           <br/>
           <br/>
           "Ohhhh, the part that was so bad."
           <br/>
           <br/>
           "YES."
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <div style="text-align:center">
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017yf24/">
             <img alt="" src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017yf24/s320x320" width="250"/>
            </a>
            <a href="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017zr0e/">
             <img alt="" src="http://pics.livejournal.com/cleolinda/pic/0017zr0e/s320x320" width="250"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           I like how they give you both "TRUST ME" and "I TRUST YOU" (asked and answered!). "U R MY LIFE" needs a "LOL" at the end, though, I think.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           How about the taste? (Note: Orange and purple ~*sparkle*~. Or kind of look like they've come down with a metallic rash. Whichever, that's cool.)
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <b>
            Secret Strawberry:
           </b>
           Ever so vaguely like strawberry bubblegum. Not bad. Wouldn't fight you for it, but I wouldn't turn it down, either. Actually, I went back to this one after I'd tested the other three.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <b>
            ~*Orange Obsession*~:
           </b>
           Very distinctly orange (I mean, considering that it's a bland, chalky candy). Kind of a popsicle-type orange. "Sparkles" are only on the outside, however.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <b>
            ~*Passion Fruit*~:
           </b>
           Suggestive of grapefruit and something else, I can't tell what--a touch of raspberry (maybe that's the sparkle)? I don't know offhand what passion fruit tastes like, so I can't really judge. Would not eat again.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <b>
            Tempting Apple:
           </b>
           So vaguely, vaguely red that you can hardly tell it apart from the strawberry. (Ah! Here's the secret: it's red once you take it out of your mouth.) (That's what she said.) (I'm sorry, I won't do that again.) Tastes like it's thinking about being apple-flavored, maybe tomorrow if we feel like it. Kind of tastes like a little Passion Fruit got mixed in, I don't know. Wait, there's the apple flavor, I'm kind of getting it now. Wouldn't eat this again either.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Of course, I've never liked conversation heart candy--not to eat, anyway; I've always felt like their true calling was to be craft supplies. In fact, you know what? I think I've got some of those Dove chocolates around here somewhere to wash out the taste. You know, the ones with the little feel-good messages in the wrappers--"Chocolate feeds your soul!" or whatever. Yeah. Good times. Good, non-chalky times.
           <a name="cutid1-end">
           </a>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Also, cryptic communication: Thank you,
           <span class="ljuser i-ljuser i-ljuser-type-P " lj:user="hakojo">
            <a class="i-ljuser-profile" href="http://hakojo.livejournal.com/profile" target="_self">
             <img class="i-ljuser-userhead" src="http://l-stat.livejournal.net/img/userinfo.gif?v=17080?v=128.7"/>
            </a>
            <a class="i-ljuser-username" href="http://hakojo.livejournal.com/" target="_self">
             <b>
              hakojo
             </b>
            </a>
           </span>
           ! I think it'll show up in the next installment. : )
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <br/>

             Forks is the name of the town. The rainiest, most overcast town in the history of ever, hence a magnet for sparklepires, etc. It's the one you give to the kid in class you don't like, I guess.
            </div>

            <div class="comment-text">
             I think the movie tie-in food item I miss most is the Pirates of the Caribbean White Chocolate (or were they vanilla?) M&amp;Ms. (They called them pearls.)
             <br/>
             THOSE THINGS WERE AMAZING. They were my favorite movie snack that entire summer.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             My friend bought me the RPattz box as a joke. I had wondered whether or not they were like the actual chalky conversation hearts, or maybe a tastier version. And now I know... and I think I'll just keep the box as a funny momento.

             Oh, hey - I thought you might find this amusing, and this seems like an appropriate entry to mention it in.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             At my school, there's this four-part poster up in the hallway outside one teacher's classroom. It has been there pretty much all year. It basically has pictures of Edward and Bella being woobly and the Twilight cast being attractive on it, and descriptions of each book.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             A friend and I have decided that it needs some new pictures. Our choices?
             <a href="http://i41.tinypic.com/15odwy8.gif" rel="nofollow">
              This one
             </a>
             for the Twilight portion and
             <a href="http://i40.tinypic.com/24oalxj.jpg" rel="nofollow">
              this one
             </a>
             (I sloppily added the Bella head, demon-alien head already included) for the Breaking Dawn portion. Operation LOL goes down tomorrow at lunch, when the halls are deserted. Pictures will be taken.

             <div class="comment-upic">

              <p>
               <span class="ljuser i-ljuser i-ljuser-type-P " lj:user="nyahu">
                <a class="i-ljuser-profile" href="http://nyahu.livejournal.com/profile" target="_self">

              <p>
               <a class="comment-permalink" href="http://cleolinda.livejournal.com/768604.html?thread=43342172#t43342172">
                <span title="33 minutes after journal entry, 2009-04-22 08:28 pm (nyahu's time)">
                 2009-04-23 03:28 am (UTC)
                </span>
               </a>
               <span class="comment-controls">
               </span>
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="comment-text">
             Oh good.. I don't have to buy these for myself out of curiosity, now.  Thanks!
             <br/>
             <br/>
             I saw them at the store and just started flailing with my jaw open like I discovered Alice was related to a flamingo. My friend had to drag me away from the display before anyone noticed (too late).
